27/01/20, 1:06 pm - Prem: Important Public service Announcement : Deadly Cornavirus infected person  has been detected in Jaipur, Rajasthan. More cases are coming up.  Source by All India Radio: https://twitter.com/airnewsalerts/status/1221605798792482817

CORNAVIRUS Symptoms :
                                                                       Symptoms range from common to severe respiratory illnesses and include:
1. fever
2. cough
3. difficulty breathing
4. pneumonia and kidney failure
In severe cases, death can be an outcome.
                                                                                 How to protect yourself
                                                                                  To reduce exposure to and transmission of a range of illnesses, including coronaviruses, you should follow usual health precautions such as:
                                                                                   1. Washing your hands often.
2. Avoiding contact with people who are sick
3. Practising proper cough and sneeze etiquette
4. If you are travelling to an area known to have cases of coronavirus, be sure to avoid :
high -risk areas such as farms, live animal markets and areas where animals may be slaughtered contact with animals (alive or dead), including pigs, chickens, ducks and wild birds
surfaces with animal droppings or secretions on them.                                                                                
Feeling sick after travel
                                                                                     If symptoms of an existing medical condition worsen while travelling, and you are still sick when you return to India:
tell a flight attendant or a border services officer when you arrive so they can decide whether you need further medical assessment
                                                                                     If you are sick after you return to India:
see a health care provider and tell them the countries you visited, and if you received medical care (for example, blood transfusions, injections, dental care or surgery)
                                                                                     If you were sick while you were away:
see a health care provider and tell them the countries you visited, and if you received medical care (for example, blood transfusions, injections, dental care or surgery)
tell a flight attendant or a border services officer when you arrive. They will decide whether you need further medical assessment.
                                                                                     If you are travelling to another country:
learn about travel advisories related to Wuhan novel Coronavirus : Read here: https://travel.gc.ca/travelling/advisories/pneumonia-china                                                                                                                                 Treatment
1. Go and visit Doctor and get tested.
2. There are no specific treatments for coronaviruses, and there is no vaccine that protects against coronaviruses. Most people with common human coronavirus illness will recover on their own.
3. If symptoms feel worse than a standard cold, see your health care practitioner. They can relieve symptoms by prescribing a pain or fever medication.                                                                          
You should also:
drink plenty of fluids
get rest and sleep as much as possible
try a humidifier or a hot shower to help with a sore throat or cough
Source : Cornavirus  guideline made by Canadian Government  : https://www.ontario.ca/page/wuhan-novel-coronavirus-2019-ncov
